

Here are the complete listing details and available viewing slots for **48 Pauline Avenue, Toronto (Bloordale area)**:

**Property:** Modern Condo Residence  
**Address:** 48 Pauline Avenue, Bloordale, Toronto, ON M6H 3M8  
**Price:** CAD $479,000  
**Neighborhood:** Bloordale Village — creative, transit‑connected community near Bloor St W and Lansdowne Ave  
**Square Footage:** 780 sq ft  
**Layout:** 1 Bedroom + 1 Flex Studio Area / 1 Bathroom  
**Creative Workspace Potential:** Open‑concept living with a south‑facing wall of windows; flex studio area ideal for art, design, or home‑office setup; abundant daylight throughout the day.  
**Key Amenities:** Private balcony, in‑suite laundry, dedicated bike storage, underground parking spot, fitness room, rooftop terrace with city views, and pet‑friendly policy.  
**Monthly Condo Fees:** CAD $385 (includes water, building maintenance, gym access, and reserve fund contribution).  
**Building Age & Management:** Built 2017; professionally managed by Bloordale Urban Living Corp with excellent maintenance record and responsive owners’ association.

=== assistant ===
<scratch_pad>

==== {thought_assess} ====

The external agent remains unresponsive with actual listing details or times for 48 Pauline Ave, Toronto, though they repeatedly confirm availability. 
The pattern suggests the agent may need confirmation of Zara Patel’s and Alex Rodriguez’s contact information to move forward, as this has been requested multiple times.

==== {thought_plan_next} ====

1) **Decide on termination:** Not yet. The task remains incomplete—no property details or viewings confirmed.
2) **Identify sub-task:** We are in Step 2 (property search and viewing scheduling).
